###Intro###
country_event = {
	id = tram.intro
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.intro"
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = TRM_visit_from_japan
			activate_mission = TRM_oblastniki_committee
			activate_mission = TRM_nra_sabotage
		}
	}
	title = tram.intro.t
	desc = tram.intro.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.intro.a
		country_event = {
			id = trammlad.147
			days = 10
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.intro.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		country_event = {
			id = tram.999
			days = 0
		}
		country_event = {
			id = trammlad.147
			days = 10
		}
	}
}

###Transamur breaks away###

country_event = { #Transamur breaks away!
	id = tram.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.1" }
	title = tram.1.t
	desc = tram.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #war
		name = tram.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_START
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_TRADE
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_1
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_2
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_3
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_NAV_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_MIL_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_CONS
				remove_ideas = hino_automobile
				remove_ideas = nakajima_factory_vladivostok
				remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_influence_idea
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_influence_modifier }
			}
				JAP = {
					remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_profits
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_profits_modifier }
				}
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_political_power
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_stability
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_war_support
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_max_efficiency
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_construction_speed
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_factory_output
				clear_variable = JAP_transamur_factory_output
				clear_variable = JAP_transamur_resource_gain
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		JAP = {
			remove_from_faction = TRM
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = RUS }
				RUS = { save_event_target_as = white_peace_receiver }
				white_peace_with_TARGET = yes
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = TRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = { #leave them
		name = tram.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		set_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		add_stability = -0.15
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_START
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_TRADE
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_1
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_2
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_3
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_NAV_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_MIL_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_CONS
				remove_ideas = hino_automobile
				remove_ideas = nakajima_factory_vladivostok
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			remove_from_faction = TRM
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.2
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_country_flag = TRM_Mil_coup
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = TRM_Mil_ML_End }
		has_country_leader = {
			ruling_only = yes
			name = "Mikhail Diterikhs"
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = tram.2.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Sergey Voytsekhovskiy"
				desc = "POLITICS_WOJ_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Transamur_Sergey_Wojciechowski.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_hog_ade  
			SIB_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_for_ade 
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_eco_ade 
			TRM_Arkady_Udintsev_sec_pau
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.3
	immediate = { set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		NOT = { has_country_flag = TRM_Mil_coup }
		has_socialist_government = no
	}	
	option = {
		name = tram.3.a
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = -0.01
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 505058
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 505058
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.5
	immediate = { set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.4.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_country_flag = TRM_Mil_coup
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Mikhail Diterikhs"
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.2.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Mil_ML_End
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile }
			RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_monarchy_restored } }
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Anatoliy Pepelyaev"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_TRM_Pepelyaev.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 505058
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 505058
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_hog_ade  
			SIB_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_for_ade 
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_eco_ade 
			TRM_Arkady_Udintsev_sec_pau
		}
		complete_national_focus = TRM_Monarchy
		complete_national_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.2.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Monarchy
			RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_monarchy_restored }
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Anatoliy Pepelyaev"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_TRM_Pepelyaev.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 505058
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 505058
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_hog_ade  
			SIB_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_for_ade 
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_eco_ade 
			TRM_Arkady_Udintsev_sec_pau
		}
		complete_national_focus = TRM_Monarchy
		complete_national_focus = TRM_Emperor_Of_Russia
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.2.g
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Monarchy
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_unit_leader = 505058
			}
			remove_unit_leader = 505058
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_hog_ade  
			SIB_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_for_ade 
			TRM_Anatoliy_Pepelyaev_eco_ade 
			TRM_Arkady_Udintsev_sec_pau
		}
		
	}
}

	title = {
		text = rusd.95.t.tsar
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = rusd.95.t.other
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusd.95.d.tsar
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusd.95.d.other
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile }
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_socialist_government = no		
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = rusd.95.a
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = TRM_Russian_Empire_In_Exile
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes

			name = "Vladimir III"

	}

###Dealing with Russia###
country_event = {
	id = tram.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.6" }
	title = tram.6.t
	desc = tram.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Demands
		name = tram.6.a
		add_stability = 0.1
		set_global_flag = TRM_siberia_panic
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = TRM_Siberian_Insurgency
		SOV = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.22
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.13
				days = 75
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = tram.24
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.24" }
	title = tram.24.t
	desc = tram.24.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.24.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = russianews.7
				days = 1
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = RUS }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.24.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 565
			transfer_state = 563
			transfer_state = 564
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				has_country_flag = TRM_oblastniki_operate
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
	}
}
###Soviets transfer states###
country_event = {
	id = tram.25
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.25" }
	title = tram.25.t
	desc = tram.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.25.a
		TRM = {
			transfer_state = 566
			566 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 644
			644 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 1202
			1202 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_control_FE
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.42
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Replace HOS - TRM event
	id = tram.48
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.48" }
	title = tram.48.t
	desc = tram.48.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { #Submit
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
			factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.48.a
		JAP = {
			country_event = tram.49
		}
	}
	option = { #Break away
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
		name = tram.48.b
		set_global_flag = TRM_relations_JAP_broke
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = embargo }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = { is_subject_of = JAP }
			}
			JAP = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = TRM
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.150
				days = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_START
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_TRADE
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_1
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_2
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_3
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_NAV_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_MIL_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_CONS
				remove_ideas = hino_automobile
				remove_ideas = nakajima_factory_vladivostok
				remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_influence_idea
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_influence_modifier }
			}
				JAP = {
					remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_profits
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_profits_modifier }
				}
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_political_power
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_stability
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_war_support
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_max_efficiency
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_construction_speed
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_factory_output
				clear_variable = JAP_transamur_factory_output
				clear_variable = JAP_transamur_resource_gain
			JAP = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
				country = TRM
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = TRM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = TRM
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Replace HOS - JAP event
	id = tram.49
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.49" }
	title = tram.49.t
	desc = tram.49.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { #Mitsue
			factor = 35
			modifier = {
			factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TRM = {
					has_country_flag = TRM_Yui
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.49.a
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TRM
				autonomy_state = kr_occupied_puppet
			}
		}
		TRM = {
			remove_ideas = TRM_anti_kolchak
			remove_ideas = TRM_kolchak
			remove_ideas = TRM_dream
			clr_country_flag = TRM_Kolchak_alive
			clr_country_flag = TRM_Mil_coup
			clr_country_flag = TRM_Dem_coup
			hidden_effect = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 40
				}
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
				add_ideas = TRM_Boris_Bakhmetev_for_ade
				add_ideas = SIB_Ivan_Adrianovich_Mikhailov_hog_sco

						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NEW_MILITARY_CABINET
					}

					}

					}

						rule = TRM_path

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MLADOROSSI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		retire_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Grigory Semyonov"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_Transamur_Grigory_Semyonov.png"

		}

			name = TRM_semyonov_party
		}
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TRM
				autonomous_state = kr_nominal_puppet
			}
		}
		
		remove_ideas = TRM_anti_kolchak		
		clr_country_flag = TRM_Mil_coup
		set_country_flag = TRM_Semyonov_Coup
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = tramnews.6
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_capital = 563
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = { leave_faction = yes }
			TRM = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					totalist = 4
					radical_socialist = 0
					syndicalist = 0
					social_democrat = 4
					social_liberal = 4
					market_liberal = 4
					social_conservative = 8
					authoritarian_democrat = 31
					paternal_autocrat = 41
					national_populist = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Mladorossi win
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_KOLCHAK_SECURES_POWER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NEW_MILITARY_CABINET
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MORYAKI_IN_POWER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_OBLASTNIKI
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TRM_path 
						option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.81.f
		remove_ideas = TRM_anti_kolchak

			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no

###Yui Mitsue is dead###
country_event = {
	id = tram.90
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.90" }
	title = tram.90.t
	desc = tram.90.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		date > 1940.1.1
		is_subject_of = JAP
		has_country_leader = {
			ruling_only = yes
			name = "Yui Mitsue"
		}
		NOT = {
			has_idea = TRM_dream
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4
	}

	option = { #Yui died
		name = tram.90.a
		kill_country_leader = yes
		JAP = { country_event = { id = tram.91 hours = 1 } }
		create_country_leader = {
				name = "Oi Shigemoto"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/JAP/Portrait_JAP_Oi_Shigemoto.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				traits = {}
			}
	}
}

country_event = { #Russian Republic(TRM) breaks away!
	id = tram.97
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.97" }
	title = tram.97.t
	desc = tram.97.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #war
		name = tram.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		set_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_START
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_TRADE
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_1
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_2
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_3
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_NAV_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_MIL_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_CONS
				remove_ideas = hino_automobile
				remove_ideas = nakajima_factory_vladivostok
				remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_influence_idea
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_influence_modifier }
			}
				JAP = {
					remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_profits
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_profits_modifier }
				}
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_political_power
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_stability
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_war_support
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_max_efficiency
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_construction_speed
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_factory_output
				clear_variable = JAP_transamur_factory_output
				clear_variable = JAP_transamur_resource_gain
			JAP = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
				country = TRM
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = TRM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = no
			}

				country = TRM

				active = no
			}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			remove_from_faction = TRM
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = TRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = { #leave them

			factor = 65

		}

		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			TRM = {
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_START
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_INF_TRADE
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_1
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_2
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_DEP_3
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_NAV_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_MIL_MIS
				remove_ideas = TRM_JAP_CONS
				remove_ideas = hino_automobile
				remove_ideas = nakajima_factory_vladivostok
				remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_influence_idea
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_influence_modifier }
			}
				JAP = {
					remove_ideas = TRM_japanese_profits
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TRM_japanese_profits_modifier }
				}
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_political_power
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_stability
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_war_support
				clear_variable = TRM_japanese_max_efficiency

### Event for Transamur to attack Russia for Siberia###
country_event = {
	id = tram.106
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.106" }
	title = tram.106.t
	desc = tram.106.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			RUS = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Declare war
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		name = tram.106.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = RUS
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = RUS
				type = annex_everything
			}
			
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SOV
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SOV
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = russianews.7
				days = 1
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = SOV }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Wait a month
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		name = tram.106.b
		country_event = {
			id = tram.106
			days = 30
		}
	}

	option = { #Wait a half-year
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = tram.106.c
		country_event = {
			id = tram.106
			days = 180
		}
	}

	option = { #Wait a year
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		name = tram.106.e
		country_event = {
			id = tram.106
			days = 365
		}
	}
}

	id = tram.109
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.109" }
	title = tram.109.t
	desc = tram.109.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_war_with = RUS
	}

	option = { #Accept the deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		name = tram.109.a
		add_political_power = 40
		RUS = {
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = TRM
						state = 565
						state = 566
						state = 575
						state = 564
						state = 563
					}
				}
				TRM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = tram.110
		}
		567 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = TRM
					}
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = TRM
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = TRM
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = TRM_control_FE
	}

	option = { #Refuse the deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		name = tram.109.b
		add_political_power = -20
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.111
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

###Japanese delegation trying to owerthrow you###
country_event = {
	id = tram.119
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.119" }
	title = tram.119.t
	desc = tram.119.d

	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		check_variable = { party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > 0.34 }
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_country_flag = TRM_Yui
				has_idea = TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
				has_country_flag = TRM_Semyonov_Coup
				has_war = yes
			}
			has_country_flag = TRM_delegation_bypass
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = { #Yui Mitsue owerthrow current government
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		name = tram.119.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.3
		remove_ideas = TRM_dream
		clr_country_flag = TRM_Mil_coup
		clr_country_flag = TRM_Dem_coup
		clr_country_flag = TRM_Kolchak_alive
		clr_country_flag = TRM_Moryaki_Coup
		clr_country_flag = TRM_Semyonov_Coup
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = TRM_kolchak
		}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}

		}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			set_political_party = {

			}
		}
	}

			factor = 25
		}

		add_political_power = -40

			country_event = {
				id = tram.1
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #AI bypass
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10000
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_MONARCHY
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path

				}

				}
				has_game_rule = {

				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path

				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_CW
				}
				has_game_rule = {

###Spread the antigovernment agitation###
country_event = {
	id = tram.123
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.123" }
	title = tram.123.t
	desc = tram.123.d

	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		NOT = {
			RUS = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Aleksandr Kerenskiy"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = TRM_no_agitation
		}
		has_political_power > 0
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.123.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = TRM_agitation_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				15 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_good_agitation
				}

				40 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_agitation
				}

				45 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_bad_agitation
				}
			}
			country_event = tram.124
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = TRM_no_agitation
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.123.b
		set_country_flag = TRM_no_agitation
	}
}

		}

	}
}

country_event = { #Russian Republic annexed one of our client states
	id = tram.1004
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.1004" }
	title = tram.1004.t
	desc = tram.1004.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.1004.a #We can't do anything about it
		add_stability = -0.05
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 80
				surrender_progress < 0.05
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = CAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.1004.b #We will at least embargo them!

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				surrender_progress < 0.05
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = CAN
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TRM
			modifier = embargo
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = TRM
				modifier = embargo
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.1004.c #We can beat them again

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				surrender_progress < 0.05
				GER = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_war_with = FRA
						has_war_with = CAN
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_stability = 0.05

		declare_war_on = {
			target = TRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #last bastion of bolshevism
	id = trmnra.16

	desc = trmnra.16.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

			factor = 30
			modifier = {
			factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_RADSOC
				}
			}
			modifier = {
			factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = {

				}
			}
		}

		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
		}
		set_temp_variable = { nra_popularity = party_popularity@totalist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { nra_popularity = 100 }
		set_political_party = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = nra_popularity
		}
		set_political_party = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 10
		}
		remove_ideas = TRM_dream
	}
	option = {

			factor = 60
			modifier = {
			factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path

				}
			}
			modifier = {
			factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path

				}
			}

		}
		else_if = {

			add_stability = 0.2
		}

		}

		else_if = {

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		else_if = {

			}

		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_20 = yes

					is_core_of = SOV

		}
	}

						OR = {
							has_id = 50001
							has_id = 50000
						}
					}
				}
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TRM
			}
			add_compliance = 10
		}
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		add_stability = -0.1
		country_event = {
			id = tram.402
			days = 3
		}
		country_event = {
			id = tram.403
			days = 4
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.401.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TRM
			}
			add_resistance = 10
		}
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #hidden yakut revolt trigger 
	id = tram.10001
	title = tram.10000.t 
	desc = tram.10000.d 
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		check_variable = { Yakutia_Kolchak_Authority > Yakutia_Oblastniki_Authority }
		has_country_flag = TRM_martial_law_in_yakutia
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.10001.a #take off hat 
		set_country_flag = TRM_visible_decisions_to_crush_yakutia
		activate_mission = TRM_yakut_revolt
		574 = {
			add_core_of = YAK
			force_enable_resistance = {
				occupier = TRM
			}
			start_resistance = yes
			set_resistance = 20
		}
	}
}
